Western and southern Anatolia, which have a <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_climate" title="Mediterranean climate">Mediterranean climate</a>, contain <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_forests,_woodlands,_and_scrub" title="Mediterranean forests, woodlands, and scrub">Mediterranean forests, woodlands, and scrub</a> ecoregions.\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Euxine-Colchic_deciduous_forests" title="Euxine-Colchic deciduous forests">Euxine-Colchic deciduous forests</a>: These temperate broadleaf and mixed forests extend across northern Anatolia, lying between the mountains of northern Anatolia and the Black Sea. They include the enclaves of <a href="/wiki/Temperate_rainforest" title="Temperate rainforest">temperate rainforest</a> lying along the southeastern coast of the Black Sea in eastern Turkey and Georgia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Northern_Anatolian_conifer_and_deciduous_forests" title="Northern Anatolian conifer and deciduous forests">Northern Anatolian conifer and deciduous forests</a>: These forests occupy the mountains of northern Anatolia, running east and west between the coastal Euxine-Colchic forests and the drier, continental climate forests of central and eastern Anatolia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Central Anatolian deciduous forests: These forests of deciduous oaks and evergreen pines cover the plateau of central Anatolia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Central Anatolian <a href="/wiki/Steppe" title="Steppe">steppe</a>: These dry grasslands cover the drier valleys and surround the saline lakes of central Anatolia, and include <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Halophytic" title="Halophytic">halophytic</a> (salt tolerant) plant communities.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Eastern Anatolian deciduous forests: This ecoregion occupies the plateau of eastern Anatolia. The drier and more continental climate is beneficial for steppe-forests dominated by deciduous oaks, with areas of shrubland, montane forest, and valley forest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Anatolian conifer and deciduous mixed forests: These forests occupy the western, Mediterranean-climate portion of the Anatolian plateau. Pine forests and mixed pine and oak woodlands and shrublands are predominant.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Aegean and Western Turkey sclerophyllous and mixed forests: These Mediterranean-climate forests occupy the coastal lowlands and valleys of western Anatolia bordering the Aegean Sea. The ecoregion has forests of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkish_pine" title="Turkish pine">Turkish pine</a> <i>(Pinus brutia)</i>, oak forests and woodlands, and <a href="/wiki/Maquis_shrubland" title="Maquis shrubland">maquis shrubland</a> of Turkish pine and evergreen <a href="/wiki/Sclerophyll" title="Sclerophyll">sclerophyllous</a> trees and shrubs, including <a href="/wiki/Olive" title="Olive">Olive</a> <i>(Olea europaea)</i>, <a href="/wiki/Arbutus_unedo" title="Arbutus unedo">Strawberry Tree</a> <i>(Arbutus unedo)</i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Arbutus_andrachne" title="Arbutus andrachne">Arbutus andrachne</a></i>, Kermes Oak <i>(<a href="/wiki/Quercus_coccifera" title="Quercus coccifera">Quercus coccifera</a>)</i>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bay_Laurel" title="Bay Laurel">Bay Laurel</a> <i>(Laurus nobilis)</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup></li>\n<li>Southern Anatolian montane conifer and deciduous forests: These mountain forests occupy the Mediterranean-climate <a href="/wiki/Taurus_Mountains" title="Taurus Mountains">Taurus Mountains</a> of southern Anatolia. Conifer forests are predominant, chiefly Anatolian black pine <i>(<a href="/wiki/Pinus_nigra" title="Pinus nigra">Pinus nigra</a>)</i>, Cedar of Lebanon <i>(<a href="/wiki/Cedrus_libani" title="Cedrus libani">Cedrus libani</a>)</i>, Taurus fir <i>(<a href="/wiki/Abies_cilicica" title="Abies cilicica">Abies cilicica</a>)</i>, and <a href="/wiki/Juniper" title="Juniper">juniper</a> <i>(<a href="/wiki/Juniperus_foetidissima" title="Juniperus foetidissima">Juniperus foetidissima</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Juniperus_excelsa" title="Juniperus excelsa">J. excelsa</a>)</i>. Broadleaf trees include oaks, <a href="/wiki/Hornbeam" title="Hornbeam">hornbeam</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Maple" title="Maple">maples</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Eastern_Mediterranean_conifer-sclerophyllous-broadleaf_forests" title="Eastern Mediterranean conifer-sclerophyllous-broadleaf forests">Eastern Mediterranean conifer-sclerophyllous-broadleaf forests</a>: This ecoregion occupies the coastal strip of southern Anatolia between the Taurus Mountains and the Mediterranean Sea. Plant communities include broadleaf sclerophyllous maquis shrublands, forests of Aleppo Pine <i>(</i>Pinus halepensis<i>)</i> and Turkish Pine <i>(Pinus brutia)</i>, and dry oak <i>(Quercus</i> spp.) woodlands and steppes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">Demographics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Anatolia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Demographics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Demographics_of_Turkey" title="Demographics of Turkey">Demographics of Turkey</a></div>\n<p>Almost 80% of the people currently residing in Anatolia are <a href="/wiki/Turkish_people" title="Turkish people">Turks</a>. <a href="/wiki/Kurds" title="Kurds">Kurds</a> constitute a major community in southeastern Anatolia,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> and are the largest ethnic minority. <a href="/wiki/Abkhazians" title="Abkhazians">Abkhazians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albanians" title="Albanians">Albanians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arabs" title="Arabs">Arabs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arameans" title="Arameans">Arameans</a>, <a href="/wiki/Armenians" title="Armenians">Armenians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Assyrian_people" title="Assyrian people">Assyrians</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Azerbaijani_people" title="Azerbaijani people">Azerbaijanis</a>, Bosnian Muslims, <a href="/wiki/Circassians" title="Circassians">Circassians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gagauz_people" title="Gagauz people">Gagauz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Georgians" title="Georgians">Georgians</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serbs" title="Serbs">Serbs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greeks" title="Greeks">Greeks</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hemshin_people" title="Hemshin people">Hemshin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jews" title="Jews">Jews</a>, <a href="/wiki/Laz_people" title="Laz people">Laz</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Levantines" title="Levantines">Levantines</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomaks" title="Pomaks">Pomaks</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zaza_people" title="Zaza people">Zazas</a> and a number of other ethnic groups also live in Anatolia in smaller numbers.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">Cuisine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Anatolia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Cuisine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Bamia" title="Bamia">Bamia</a> is a traditional Anatolian-era stew dish prepared using <a href="/wiki/Lamb_and_mutton" title="Lamb and mutton">lamb</a>, <a href="/wiki/Okra" title="Okra">okra</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tomatoes" title="Tomatoes">tomatoes</a> as primary ingredients.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Anatolia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24"
